<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>ве́ртел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vértel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>ве́ртела</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>вертела́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертел.html>вертело́в</a></b>)

***вертеп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́п</a> (29867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вьртьпъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vĭrtĭpŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave, garden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́п</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertép</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">врътъпъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vrŭtŭpŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave, garden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">върто́п</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vǎrtóp</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whirlpool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">vrtèp</i>. Per Brandt, a borrowing from Church Slavonic. Per Vasmer, possibly related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">вр̏т</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">vérti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">veriù</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tocharian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Tocharian languages">Tocharian B</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="txb">warto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garden, grove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="txb">wärto</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">weorð</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house fence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">worð</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vertép</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеп.html>верте́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cave, hideout</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> den, lair <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially of criminals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukraine" class="extiw" title="w:Ukraine">Ukraine</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> large box for puppets displaying nativity scenes or comic scenes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> performance of such puppets</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***вертеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a> (7251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьrtěti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wert-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vertétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повертеть.html>поверте́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn, to twist, to twirl, to spin</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеться.html>верте́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vertétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повертеться.html>поверте́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn around, to revolve, to spin</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***вертикально.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вертикальный.html>вертика́льно</a> (14175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертикальный.html>вертика́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertikálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертикальный.html>вертика́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vertikálʹno</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертеть.html>верте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертушка.html>верту́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vertúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертушка.html>верту́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертушка.html>верту́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вертушка.html>верту́шек</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">верту́н</b>)

<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">

***верх.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a> (2408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьrxъ</i> (whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">врьхъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vrĭxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wers-</i>.
</p><p>Balto-Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">viršus</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">virsus</i>. Other Indo-European cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">verruca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a steep place, height</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἕρμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hérma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reef, rock, hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">verx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>ве́рха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верхи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верхо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>top, upper part, roof, dome, height</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> summit, apex
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совещание.html>совеща́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верха́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soveščánije v <b>verxáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">summit meeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>the highest degree of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́пости</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto <b>verx</b> glúposti!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is the height of stupidity!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">verx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>ве́рха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верха́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верхо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>right side (of clothing, fabric), shoe upper, boot top</li>
<li>hood, top, soft top, rag top of a carriage or convertible automobile</li>
<li>cap, cover, outside, shell (clothing, as opposed to a lining)</li></ol>

***вершина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́на</a> (1661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veršína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>peak, top, summit
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1966</b>,  “Вершина  | The Summit | ”, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Vysotsky" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vladimir Vysotsky">Владимир Высоцкий</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>ру́бим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ступень.html>ступе́ни</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>Ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>ша́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>!<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> напряже́нья <a href = vnd.unilang:колено.html>коле́ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрожать.html>дрожа́т</a>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>груди́</a>.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>Весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́ни</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счастливый.html>сча́стлив</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́м</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:немного.html>немно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завидовать.html>зави́дуешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́м</a>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́м</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впереди.html>впереди́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My rúbim stupéni. Ni šágu nazád!<br />I ot naprjažénʹja koléni drožát,<br />I sérdce gotóvo k <b>veršíne</b> bežátʹ iz grudí.<br />Vesʹ mír na ladóni - ty sčástliv i ném<br />I tólʹko nemnógo zavíduješʹ tém,<br />Drugím - u kotóryx <b>veršína</b> ješčó vperedí.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We are chopping steps. Not one step back!<br />And from the pressure our knees are shaking,<br />And our hearts are ready to run out of our chests to <b>the summit</b>.<br />The whole world is in the palm of your hand - you are happy and mute<br />And are envying just a little those<br />Others for whom <b>the summit</b> is still ahead.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>acme, height</li>
<li>vertex, apex</li></ol>

***вершить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вершить.html>верши́ть</a> (22795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьršiti</i>, cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">върше́я</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vǎršéja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thresh, to flail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершить.html>верши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veršítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свершить.html>сверши́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поверши́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manage, to control, to direct, to do, to accomplish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вершить.html>верши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правосудие.html>правосу́дие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>veršítʹ</b> pravosúdije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to administer justice, dispense justice, mete out justice, render justice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вершить.html>верши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>су́дьбами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>veršítʹ</b> súdʹbami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rule sway the destinies</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вершить.html>верши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>veršítʹ</b> delámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to manage control, to direct affairs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вершок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вершок.html>вершо́к</a> (19099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">verx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">top</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably originally "length of the upper phalanx of the index finger".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершок.html>вершо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veršók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершок.html>вершка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершок.html>вершки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вершок.html>вершко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>an old Russian unit of length approximately equal to 4.445 centimeters or 1/16 of an arshin</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***веселеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселеть.html>веселе́ть</a> (31188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>весёлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesjólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселеть.html>веселе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veselétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повеселеть.html>повеселе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cheer up, to become merry/cheerful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселить.html>весели́ть</a> (18389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселить.html>весели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veselítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеселить.html>развесели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to amuse, to give joy, to gladden</li>
<li>to exhilarate, to rejoice</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселиться.html>весели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veselítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повеселиться.html>повесели́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеселиться.html>развесели́ться</a></b>)

***весело.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a> (1340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véselo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ве́село" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)веселе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ве́село" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:веселеть.html>веселе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>merrily, cheerfully</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостно.html>ра́достно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádostno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешной.html>смешно́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smešnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véselo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one is happy, cheerful, convivial, hilarious, merry, bright, jolly, gleeful, lighthearted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>véselo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he enjoys himself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>it is funny</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véselo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>весёлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesjólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
